the set of combination-dependent-basic-strategy tables

 
If the user-defined set of game rules does not give
the option to split to the player, then the set of
combination-dependent-basic-strategy tables consists
of one combination-dependent-basic-strategy table found
for the player non-split-initial hands.
 
If the user-defined set of game rules does give the
the option to split to the player, then the set of
combination-dependent-basic-strategy tables consists
of one combination-dependent-basic-strategy table found
for the player initial hands, and two combination-
dependent-basic-strategy tables found for the player's
post-split-initial hands.
 
Each combination-dependent-basic-strategy table is
divided into seven subtables with each subtable being
displayed on one page wherein: each row is labeled
by a set of two characters representing the first two
cards of the player's hand, wherein each column is
labeled by a set of two characters representing the
first two cards of the dealer's hand, and wherein zero
represents the rank of joker.
 
In each combination-dependent-basic-strategy subtable
found for the player's initial hands, the order of
the two cards in the player's initial hand does not
correspond to the order of the two characters
representing the hand, and the order of the two cards
in the dealer's initial hand does not correspond to the
the order of the two characters representing the hand.
 
In each combination-dependent-basic-strategy subtable
found for the player's post-split hands, the order
of the two cards in the player's post-split hand
does correspond to the order of the two characters
representing the hand, and the order of the two cards
in the dealer's initial hand does not correspond to the
the order of the two characters representing the hand.
 
A combination-dependent-basic-strategy subtable found
for the player's initial hands. It displays data about
the most favorable player responses to dealer hands 00 to AA
